                    </msIdentifier>

                    <msContents>
                        <summary xml:lang="en">
                            <p>This part of the Nepalese version of the
                                    <title>Suśrutasaṃhitā</title> is supported from
                                beginning to end by witness H.</p>
                            <p>Witness K supports SS.4.2.24 - 78, where the MS breaks off.
                                K resumes at SS.4.19.22 and continues to the end of the
                                chapter at SS.4.20.63.</p>
                            <p>Witness Kb is a single leaf that duplicates material in the
                                main manuscript K and is written by a different scribe. It
                                supports SS.4.19.44 - 4.20.30.</p>
                        </summary>


                        <msItem defective="true" n="1">

        <body>
            <div n="4" type="sthāna">

                <div n="1" type="adhyāya">

                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 1: draft based on MS H 2023-10-22]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto dvivraṇīyaṃ cikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dvau vraṇau bhavataḥ | śarīrasamutthaś cāgantuś ca tayoḥ
                        śarīrasamuttho vātapittakaphaśoṇitasannipātanimitta āgantukaḥ
                            puruṣa<pc> </pc>mṛga<pc> </pc>paśu<pc> </pc>pakṣi<pc
                            > </pc>vyāḍasarīsṛpa<pc> </pc>patanapīḍana<pc
                            > </pc>prahārāgniviṣāsthi<pc
                            > </pc>sakalakapālakhaḍga<pc> </pc>cakreṣu
                        paraśuśaktikuntādyāyudhaprahareṇābhighātanimittaḥ | tatra tulye
                        vraṇasāmānye dvikāraṇotthānaprayojanasāmarthyād dvivraṇīyaḥ ity
                        ucyate |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvvasminn eva cāgantau vraṇe tat kālam eva kṣatoṣmaṇaḥ |
                        prasṛtasyaupaśamārtham pittavacchītakriyāvibhāgaḥ | sandhānārthañ
                        ca madhughṛtopayoga iti | etad vikāraṇotthānaprayojanam
                        uttarakālan tu doṣopaplavaviśeṣā<hi>d avasthāntaraviśeṣāḥ</hi>
                        śārīravat pratīkāraḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣopaplavaviśeṣaḥ punaḥ samāsataḥ pañcadaśaprakāro bhavati |
                        yathokte vraṇapraśnādhyāye prasaraṇasāmarthyāc chaddhaś ceti
                        ṣoḍaśaprakāra ity ucyate |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasya lakṣaṇaṃ dvividhaṃ | sāmānyalakṣaṇam viśeṣalakṣaṇañ ca |
                        tatra vraṇe vṛṇotīti vraṇaḥ |
                        viśeṣalakṣaṇampunarvvātādisvalakṣaṇaviśeṣaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra śyāvāruṇābhabhastanu
                        śītapicchilālpasrāvīrūkṣaścaṭacaṭāyanaśīlaḥ sphuraṇāyām
                        atodabhedavedanābahulo nirmmāṃsaś ceti vātāt || kṣiprajaḥ
                        pītanīlābhaḥ kiṃśukodakābhoṣṇasrāvī dāhapākavikārī
                        pītapiṭakājuṣṭaś ceti pittāt || pratataḥ kaṇḍubahulaḥ sthūloṣṭhaḥ
                        stavdhasirāsnāyujālāvanaddhaḥ kaṭhinaḥ pāṇḍvāvabhāso mandavedanaḥ
                        | śuklaśītasāndrapicchilāsrāvī guruś ceti kaphāt ||
                        pravālānalanicayaprakāśaḥ
                        kṛṣṇasphoṭapiṭakājālopacitasturaṃgasthānagandhī savedanaḥ |
                        pradhūpanaśīlo raktasrā vī pittaliṅgaś ceti raktāt ||
                        pratodadāhadhūpāyanaprāyaḥ pītāruṇābhastadvarṇṇasrāvī ceti
                        vātapittābhyāṃ || kaṇḍūyanaśīlaḥ sanistodavātrūkṣaḥ kharastaddho
                        muhurmmuhuḥ śītapicchalāsrāvī ceti vātaśleṣmābhyāṃ || guruḥ
                        sadāhoṣṇaḥ pītapāṇḍusrāvī ceti pittaśleṣmābhyāṃ ||
                        tanurūkṣastodabahulaḥ prasupta iva ca kṛṣṇāruṇā
                        bhastadvvarṇṇasrāvī ceti vātaśoṇitābhyāṃ || ghṛtamaṇḍābho
                        mīnadhāvanagandhīmṛdurvvisarppīkṛṣṇoṣṇasrāvī ceti pittaśoṇitābhyāṃ
                        || rakto gurusnigdhaḥ kaṇḍūprāyaḥ picchilaḥ saraktasrāvī ceti
                        śleṣmaśoṇitābhyāṃ | sphuraṇatodadāhadhūmāyanaprāyaḥ
                        pītatanuraktasrāvī ceti vātapittaśoṇitebhyaḥ ||
                        kaṇḍūsphuraṇacumucumāyamānaprāyaḥ pāṇḍutanuraktasrāvī ceti
                        vātaśleṣmaśoṇitebhyaḥ || dāhapākarāgakaṇḍūprāyaḥ
                        pāṇḍūraktapītāsrāvī ceti pittaśleṣmaśoṇitebhyaḥ ||
                        vividhadoṣavarṇṇavedanāsrāvaviśeṣopetaḥ pavanapittakaphebhyaḥ ||
                        nirddarśakanirmmathanasphuraṇatodadāhapākarāgakaṇḍūvāṃsvāpabahulo
                        nānāvidhavarṇṇavedanāsrāvaviśeṣopetaḥ pavanapittakaphaśoṇitebhya
                        iti || jihvātalābho mṛdu ślakṣṇaḥ snigdho vigatavedanaḥ
                        suvyavasthito nirāsrāvaś ceti śuddho vraṇaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasyaitasya vraṇasya ṣaṣṭirupakramā bhavanti | tad
                        yathāpatarpaṇam ālepanaḥ pariṣeko 'bhyaṅgaḥ svedo vimlāyanam
                        upanāho visrāvaṇaṃ sneho vamanam virecanaṃ | cchedyaṃ
                        bhedyandāraṇaṃ lekhya meṣyamāhāryaṃ vyadhyaṃ sevyaṃ pīḍanaṃ
                        sandhānam visrāvyaṃ śoṇitasthāpanannirvvāpaṇa mūtkārikā kaṣāyo
                        varttiḥ kalkaḥ sarppistailam piṇḍīkaraṇaṃ rasakriyācūrṇṇam
                        vraṇadhūpanamutsādanamavasādanaṃ mṛdukarmma dāruṇakarmma
                        kṣārakarmmāgnikarmma kṛṣṇakarmma pāṇḍūkarmma
                        samavarṇṇalomasañjananaṃ lomasaṃharaṇaṃ
                        bastikarmmottarabastikarmma vandhena patradānaṃ krimighnaṃ
                        vṛṃhaṇam viṣaghnaṃ śirovirecanannasyaṃ kavaladhāraṇaṃ dhūpo
                        madhusarppiryantram āhāro rakṣāvidhānam iti</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.9">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         teṣu kaṣāyo varttiḥ kalkaḥ sarppistailaṃ rasakriyācūrṇṇam iti |
                        śodhanaropaṇāni | evam ete ṣaṣṭirupakramā bhavanti || teṣv aṣṭau
                        śastrakṛtyāḥ śoṇitasthāpanaṃ kṣārāgniryantram āhāro rakṣāvidhānam
                        ity uktāḥ |
                        snehasvedavamanavirecanavastyuttarabastividhānaśirovirecanarakṣāgninasyadhūmanakavalavidhānāny
                        uttaratra vakṣyāmaḥ | yad anyad avasiṣṭam upakramajātaṃ tad atra
                        vakṣyate |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.10">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra ṣaḍvidhaḥ prādiṣṭaḥ śophastasyaikādaśopakramā bhavanti |
                        apatarppaṇādayo virecanāntāḥ | viśeṣeṇa vraṇapratīkāre varttante
                        vraṇabhāvam upagatasya na virudhyante śeṣās tu prāyeṇa
                        vraṇapratīkārahetava eva |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.11">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         apatarppaṇa ādya upakrama eṣa sarvvaśophānāṃ sāmānyataḥ
                        pradhānatamaś ca || bha ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.12">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣocchrāyopaśāntyarthandoṣānaddhasya dehinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         avekṣya doṣaṃ prāṇañ ca kāryaṃ syādapatarppaṇaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.13">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         taddhimārutakṣuttṛṣṇā mukhaśoṣasramānvite |
                        <caesura/>
                         kāryaṃ na vālavṛddhe vā na garbbhiṇyāṃ na durvvale ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.14">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śopheṣūtthitamātreṣu vraṇeṣūgrarujeṣu ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathoktairauṣadhairllepaṃ pratyekāṃśyena kārayet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.15">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā prajvalite veśmanyambhasā pariṣecanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣipraṃ praśamayatyagnimevam ālepanaṃ rujaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.16">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         prahlādane śodhane ca śophasya haraṇe tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         utsādane ropane ca lepaḥ syāt tu tadarthakṛt ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.17">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vātaśephe tu vedanopaśamārthaṃ
                        sarppistailadhānyāmlamāṃsarasavātaharauṣadhaniḥkvāthairaśītaiḥ
                        pariṣekaṃ kurvvīta | pittaraktābhighātaviṣanimitteṣu
                        kṣīravṛkṣakṣīraśarkkarodakakekṣurasaghṛtamadhurauṣadhaniḥkvāthairanuṣṇaiḥ
                        | śleṣmaśophe tu
                        tailamūtrakṣārodakasurāśuktakaphaghnauṣadhaniḥkvāthairaśītair</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.18">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yathāmvubhiḥ sicyamānaḥ śāntimagnirnniyacchati |
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣāgnirevaṃ sahasā pariṣekeṇa śāmyati ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.19">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         abhyaṅgas tu doṣam ālocyopayukto doṣopaśamo mṛdutāṃ ca karoti
                        |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.20">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         svedavimlāpanādīnāṃ kriyāṇāṃ prāk sa ucyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         paś cāt karmmasu cādiṣṭaḥ sa tu visrāvaṇādiṣu ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.21">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.21</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rujāvatāndāruṇānāṅkaṭhinānāntathaiva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         śophānāṃ svedanaṃ kāryaṃ ye cāpyevamvidhā vraṇāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.22">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.22</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sthirāṇāṃ rujatāmmandaṃ kāryaṃ vimlāpanambhavet |
                        <caesura/>
                         abhyajya svedayitvā ca veṇunāḍyā tataḥ śanaiḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.23">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.23</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vimarddayed bhiṣakprājñastalenāṅguṣṭhakena vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         śophayor upanāhan tu kuryādāmavidagdhayoḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.24">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.24</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         praśāmyaty avidagdhas tu vidagdhaḥ pākameti ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         nivarttate na yaḥ śopho virekāntair upakramaiḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.25">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.25</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra saṃpācanadravyāṇyāhṛtyoktāni pivya ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         dadhitakrasurāśuktadhānyāmlairyojayed bhiṣak ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.26">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.26</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         snigdhāni lavaṇī kṛtvā paced utkārikān tataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sairaṇḍapatrayā śophan nāhayed uṣṇayā tayā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.27">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.27</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         hitaṃ saṃbhojanañcāpi pākāya vimukho yadi |
                        <caesura/>
                         vedanopaśamārthāya tathā pākabhayāya ca ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.28">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.28</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         acirotpatite śophe kuryāc choṇitamokṣaṇaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         saśophe kaṭhine dhyāme sarakte vedanāvati ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.29">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.29</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃravdhe viṣame cāpi vraṇe viśrāvaṇaṃ hitaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.30">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.30</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sopadravādravāṇāṃ rūkṣāṇāṅkṛśānāṃ vraṇaśoṣiṇāṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.31">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.31</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā svauṣadhasaṃsiddhaṃ snehapānamvidhīyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         utsannamāṃsaśophe tu kaphe duṣṭe viśeṣataḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.32">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.32</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃsṛṣṭadhyāmarudhire vraṇe praccharddanaṃ hitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vātapittapraduṣṭeṣu dīrghakālānuvandhiṣu ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.33">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.33</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         virecanampraśaṃsanti vraṇeṣu vraṇakovidāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         apākavatsurogeṣu kaṭhineṣu sthireṣu ca ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.34">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.34</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         snāyukothādiṣu tathā cchedanaṃ prāptam ucyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         antaḥ pūyeṣv avaktreṣu tathaivotsaṅgavatsv api||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.35">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.35</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         gatimatsu ca rogeṣu bhedanamprāptamucyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         vālavṛddhakṣatakṣīṇabhīrūṇāṃ yoṣitām api ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.36">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.36</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         marmmopari ca jāteṣu rogeṣūktañ ca dāruṇaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         supakve piṇḍite śophe pīḍanair upapīḍite ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.37">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.37</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pākoddhateṣu doṣeṣu tat tu kāryam vijānatā |
                        <caesura/>
                         supiṣṭairdāraṇadravyaiḥ ṛtakṣāraṇa vā punaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.38">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.38</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṭhinasthūlavattauṣṭhān dīryamānān punaḥ punaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṭhinātsannamāṃsām̐ś ca lekhanair ācared bhiṣak ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.39">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.39</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         samaṃ likhetsulikhitaṃ likhen niravaśeṣataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         carmmaṇān tu pramāṇena samaṃ śastreṇa saṃlikhet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.40">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.40</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣaumaṃ plotaṃ picuṃ phenaṃ yāvaśūkaṃ sasaindhavaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         karkaśāni ca patrāṇi lekhanārthe pradāpayet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.41">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.41</label>
                        <caesura/>

                         patrāṇi kṣīravṛkṣāṇāmaudakānāntathaiva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         dūṣite raktapittābhyāmvraṇe dadyādvicakṣaṇaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.115">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.115</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pāṭhāmūrvvāś ca gandhānāṃ kākamācīharidrayoḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         patraṃ śukanasāyāś ca yojayet kaphaje vraṇe ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.116">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.116</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         akarkkaśamavicchinnamajīrṇṇamviṣavarjjitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ajan tu jagdham mṛdu ca patraṃ guṇavad ucyate ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.117">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.117</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sneham auṣadhasāram vā paṭṭapatrāntarīkṛtaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tad dadāti yatas tasmād auṣadhopari dāpayet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.118">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.118</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śītoṣṇajananārthāya snehasaṃgrahaṇāya ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         dattauṣadheṣu dātavyam patraṃ vaidyena jānatā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.119">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.119</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         makṣikāvraṇamāgatya nikṣipanti yadā krimiṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śvayathurbbhakṣite tais tu jāyate bhṛśadāruṇaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.120">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.120</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tīvrā rujo vicitrāś ca raktasrāvaṃ sravedapi |
                        <caesura/>
                         svasurasādihitas tatra dhāvane pūraṇe tathā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.121">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.121</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         saptaparṇṇakarañjārkka nimvarājādanatvacaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         gomūtrapiṣṭā ca hitāḥ sekaḥ kṣārodakena vā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.122">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.122</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vraṇaṃ pracchādayitvā ca māṃsapeṣyām vinirharet |
                        <caesura/>
                         viṃśati krimijātīm̐s tu vakṣyāmy upari bhāgaśaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.123">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.123</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dīrghakāturāṇān tu kṛṣāṇām vraṇaśoṣiṇāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vṛṃhaṇīyo vidhiḥ kāryaḥ so 'pyagnim parirakṣatā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.124">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.124</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         viṣaduṣṭasya vijñānaṃ viṣaniścayam eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         cikitsitantu vakṣyāmi taṅkalpeṣu vibhāgaśaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.125">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.125</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṇḍūmantaḥ saśophaś ca jatrūṇopari ye vraṇāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śirovirecanaṃ teṣu vidheyaṃ vakṣyate tathā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.126">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.126</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rujāvanto 'nilāviṣṭā rūkṣā ye corddhvajatrujāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vraṇeṣu teṣu karttavyaṃ nasyaṃ snehena jānatā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.127">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.127</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣam pracyāvaṇārthāya rujādāhakṣayāya ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         jihvādantasamutthasya haraṇārtham malasya ca ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.128">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.128</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śodhano ropaṇaś caiva vraṇasya mukhajasya vai |
                        <caesura/>
                         uṣṇo vā yadi vā śītaḥ kavalagraha iṣyate ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.129">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.129</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ūrddhvajatrugatān trāgān vraṇān vā kaphavātajān |
                        <caesura/>
                         śophāsrāvarujāyuktān dhūmapānair upācaret ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.130">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.130</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣatoṣmaṇāṃ nigrahārthaṃ sandhānārthantathaiva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         sadyovraṇeṣvāyateṣu madhusarppirvvidhīyate ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.131">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.131</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         avagāḍhastvaṇumukhā ye vraṇāḥ śalyapīḍitāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nivṛttahastoddharaṇā yantraṃ teṣu vidhīyate ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.132">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.132</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         laghumātro laghuś caiva snigdhāṣṇo vahnidīpanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvvavraṇibhyo deyas tu sadāhāram vijānatā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.133">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.133</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         niśācarebhyo rakṣyas tu nityam eva kṣatāturaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         rakṣāvidhānair uddiṣṭaiḥ sadā cāpi pravakṣyate ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.134">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.134</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ṣaṇmūloṣṭaparigrāhī pañcalakṣaṇalakṣitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ṣaṣṭyāvidhānaiḥ prāpnoti caturbbhiḥ sādhyate vraṇaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.135">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.135</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         alpagranthaṃ mṛgayatā yogo yo 'lpauṣadhaḥ kṛtaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dravyāṇāṃ tu samānānāntatra vāyo na duṣyati ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.136">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.136</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         prasaṃgābhihito yo vā bahudurllabhabheṣajaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathopapatyā tatrāpi kāryam eva cikitsitaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.137"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.138"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.139"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.1.140">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.1.140</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vraṇakriyāsvimāsveva samāsoktās tu yā kriyā |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhūyo 'bhidhāsyāmy upari tathā sadyovraṇeṣu tā iti ||</l>

                    <p ana="trailer">|| dvivraṇīyaṃ cikitsitaṃ prathamaḥ ||</p>

                <div n="2" type="adhyāya">

                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 2]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athātaḥ sadyovraṇacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dhanvantarir ddharmmabhṛtām variṣṭho vāgvidām varaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         viśvāmitrātmajam ṛṣiṃ śiṣyaṃ suśrutam anvaśāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nānādhārāmukhaiḥ śastrair nnānāsthānani pātitaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavaṃti nānākṛtayo vraṇās tām̐s tva nibodha me || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         āyatāś caturasrāś ca tryasrā muṇḍalinas tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         arddhacandrapratīkāśā viśālāḥ kuṭilās tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śarāvanimnamadhyāś ca yavamadhyās tathāpare |
                        <caesura/>
                         evam prakārākṛtayo bhavanty āgantavo vraṇāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣajā vā svayambhinnā na tu vaidyanimittajāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vraṇākṛtijño hi bhiṣak na moham upagacchati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         durddarśaneṣv api bhṛśaṃ vraṇeṣu vikṛteṣv api |
                        <caesura/>
                         anekākṛtir āgantuḥ sa bhiṣagbhiḥ purātanaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.9">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         samāsato lakṣaṇataḥ ṣaḍvidhaḥ parikīrttitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         chinnam bhinnan tathā viddhaṃ kṣatam picitam eva ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.10">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ghṛṣṭam āhus tathā ṣaṣṭhan teṣām vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         tiryakcīno mṛdur vvāpi so vraṇas tv āyato bhavet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.11">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         gātrapātī na vā tad dhi chinnalakṣaṇam ucyate ||
                        <caesura/>
                         śaktikunteṣukhaḍgādiviṣāṇair āśayor hataḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.12">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yat kiñcit sravate tad dhi bhinnalakṣaṇam ucyate ||
                        <caesura/>
                         sthānāny āmāgnipakvānām mūtrasya rudhirasya ca | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.13">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         hṛduṇḍukaḥ phupphusaś ca koṣṭham ity abhidhīyate ||
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmin bhinne raktapūrṇṇe jvaro dāhaś ca jāyate | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.14">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mūtramārggagudāsyebhyo raktaṃ ghrāṇāc ca gacchati ||
                        <caesura/>
                         mūrcchādhmānatṛṣāśvāsas tv abhaktacchanda eva ca | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.15">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         viṇmūtravātasaṅgañ ca svedāsrāvo kṣiraktatā ||
                        <caesura/>
                         lohagandhitvam āsyasya gātradaurggandham eva ca | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.16"> hṛcchūlaṃ pārśvayoś cāpi viśeṣaṃ cātra me śṛṇu
                        ||
                        <caesura/>
                         āmāśayasthe rudhire rudhiraṃ charddayaty api | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.17"> ādhmānam atimātraṃ ca śūlaṃ ca bhṛśadāruṇam ||
                        <caesura/>
                         pakvāsayagate cāpi rujā gauravam eva ca | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.18"> adhaḥkāye viśeṣeṇa śītatā ca bhavanti hi ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.19"> sūkṣmāsyaṃ śalyābhihataṃ yadagandhāsayam vinā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.20"> uttuṇḍitan nirgatam vā tadviddham iti nirddiśet
                        ||
                        <caesura/>
                         nāticchinnan nātividdham ubhayor llakṣaṇānvitam | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.21"> viṣamavraṇasaṃgo yaṃ
                        <caesura/>
                         prahārapīḍanābhyān tu yadaṅgam pṛthutāṃ gataṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.22"> sāsthi tat piccitam vidyāt majjāraktapariplutaṃ
                        ||
                        <caesura/>
                         gharṣaṇād abhighātād vā yad aṅgam vigatatvacaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.23"> ūṣāsrāvānvitan tan tu ghṛṣṭam ity abhidhīyate
                        ||
                        <caesura/>
                         chinne bhinne tathā viddhe kṣate vāsṛgatisrave | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.24"> raktakṣayād atra rujāḥ karoti pavano bhṛśaṃ ||
                        snehapānaṃ hitan tatra tatseko vihitas tathā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.25">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.25</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         veśavāraiḥ sakṛśaraiḥ susnigdhaś copanāhataṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dhānyasvedāṃś ca kurvīta snigdhānyālepanāni ca ||</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.26">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.26</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vātaghnauṣadhasiddhaiś ca snehair bastir vidhīyate ||
                        <caesura/>
                         piccite ca vighṛṣṭe ca nātisravati śoṇitaṃ |</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.27">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.27</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmin na gachati bhṛśaṃ dāhaḥ pākaś ca jāyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasyoṣmaṇo nigrahārthaṃ dāhapākabhayā ya ca |</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.28">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.28</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śītam ālepanaṃ kāryam pariṣekaś śītalaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ṣaṭsveteṣu yathokteṣu chinnādiṣu samāsataḥ |</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.29">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.29</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         jñeyaṃ samarpitaṃ sarvaṃ sadyovraṇacikitsitam || ❈ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         ata ūrdhvam pravakṣyāmi chinnānān tu cikitsitaṃ |</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.30">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.30</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ye vraṇā vivṛtāḥ kecic chinnāḥ pārśvāvalamvitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tāṃ sīvyed vidhinoktena vandhīyād gāḍham eva ca |</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.31">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.31</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         karṇṇaṃ sthānādapoḍhantu sthāpayutvā yathāsthitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sīvyed yathoktaṃ tailena srotaś cāpy abhitarpayet |</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.32">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.32</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛkāṭikānte chinne tu gachaty api samīraṇe |
                        <caesura/>
                         samyaṅ niveśya vadhnīyāt sīvyec cāpi nirantaram |</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.33">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.33</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ājena sarpiṣā caivaṃ pariṣeko bhidhīyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         uttānonnaṃ samaśrnīyāc chayīta ca suyantritaḥ |</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.34">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.34</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śākhāsu tiryaksatitāṃ prahārāṃ vivṛtāṃ bhṛsaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sīvyet samyaṅ niveśyāśuḥ sandhyasthīnyanupūrvaśaḥ |</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.35">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.35</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vadhyāvellitakenāśuḥ vastāntena ghanena vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         carmaṇā goḥ phaṇo vandhaḥ kāryaś vā sahate sinā |</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.36">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.36</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pṛṣṭhe vraṇo yasya bhaved uttānañ ca śayīta ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         atonyathā corasije śayīta puruṣo vraṇe |</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.37">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.37</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         chinnāṃ niḥśeṣataḥ śākhān dagdhvā tailena buddhimāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vadhnīyāt kośavandhena prāptaṃ kuryāc ca ropaṇaṃ ||</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.38">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.38</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         candanaṃ padmakaṃ lodhram utpalādi priyaṃgavaḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         haridrā madhukaṃ caiva payaś cāṣṭamam eva tu |</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.39">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.39</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tailam ebhir vipakkaṃ syāt pradhānaṃ vraṇaropaṇaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         candanaṃ karkaṭākhyā ca sahe māṃsāhvayāmṛtā |</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.40">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.40</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         hareṇavo mṛṇālañ ca triphalā padmakotpalaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         trayodaśāṃgatrivṛtametadvā payasām ānvitaṃ |</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.41">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.41</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tailaṃ vipakvaṃ sekāryahitantu vraṇaropane || ❈ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi bhinnānān tu cikitsitaṃ |</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.42">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.42</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhinnanetramakarmaṇyamabhinnaṃ lamvate tu yaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tanniveśya yathāsthānamavyāviddhasiraṃ śanaiḥ |</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.43">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.43</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pīḍayen pāṇinā sammyak padmapatrāntareṇa tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         tatosya tarpaṇaṃ kāryan nasyañ cānena sarpiṣā |</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.44">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.44</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ajāghṛtaṃ kṣīrapātraṃ madhukañ cotpalāni ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         jīvakarsaṣabhakau cāpi piṣṭvā sarpir vipācayet |</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.45">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.45</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvanetrābhighāteṣu sarpiretat praśasyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         udarānmedaso varttirn nirgatā yasya dehinaḥ |</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.46">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.46</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tāṃ kaṣāyāvakīrṇṇan tu vadhvā sūtreṇa sūtravit |
                        <caesura/>
                         samyag chindyād vraṇena tac ca kṣaudreṇa veṣṭayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.47"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.48"/>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.49">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.49</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         acchindyamānām araṇaṃ kuryād āṭopam eva vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         medāgranthau tu yat tailaṃ vakṣyate tat tu yojayet |</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.50">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.50</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tvacotītya sirādīni bhitvā vā parihṛtya vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         kāṣṭhe pratiṣṭhitaṃ śalyaṃ kuryād uktānupadravān |</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.2.51">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.2.51</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrāntarlohitam pāṇḍuśītapādakarānanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>

                         cakrayogena matimān āñchedūrddhvasthi nirggataṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sphuṭitaṃ piccitam vāpi badhnīyāt pūrvvavad bhiṣak | </l>

                    <ab corresp="#SS.4.4.10" type="apparatus">
                        <list type="Emendation">
                            <item xml:lang="en" corresp="#SS.4.4.10-n1">We emend
                                    <foreign>karṣa</foreign> to <foreign>karṣū</foreign>
                                with the vulgate, and we emend <foreign>-bastini</foreign>
                                to <foreign>bastibhiḥ</foreign>, again with the vulgate,
                                for a meaningful text. The latter error may reflect a
                                scribal misreading of <foreign>ni</foreign> for
                                    <foreign>bhi(ḥ)</foreign> at an earlier stage of
                                transmission, since <foreign>na</foreign> and
                                    <foreign>bha</foreign> are similar in old Nepalese
                                scripts.</item>
                        </list>
                    </ab>

                         vamanaṃ hanti nasyañ ca kuśalena prayojitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śirogataṃ śirobastir hanti cāsṛg<pc> </pc>vimokṣaṇaṃ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.4.20">

                        <caesura/>
                         snehaṃ mātrāsahasran tu dhārayet tatra yogataḥ |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.4.22">

                         trivṛddantīśaṅkhinīsuvarṇṇakṣīrītriphalāviḍaṅgānām akṣasamāḥ
                        kalkā bilvamātras tilvakamūlakampillyayos triphalārasadadhipātre
                        dve dve ghṛtapātram ekan tadaikadhyam pratisaṃsṛjya vipacet
                        tilvakasarppir etat snehavirecanam upadiśanti vātarogeṣu |
                        tilvakavidhir cāśokaramyakayor draṣṭavyaḥ ||<anchor
                            n="SS.4.4.27-n1"/>
                    </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.4.28">

                        <caesura/>
                         tilapīḍanopakaraṇakāṣṭhāny āhṛtyānalpakālatailaparipīḍitāni aṇūni
                        cchedayitvāvakṣudya prakṣipya mahati kaṭāhe pānīyenāplāvya
                        kvāthayet | tatas taṃ sneham ambupṛṣthāt sarakapāṇyor
                        anyatareṇādāya vātaghnauṣadha<pc> </pc>datta<pc> </pc>pratīvāpaṃ
                        snehapākakalpena vipaced etad aṇutailam upadiśanti vātarorogeṣu
                            |<anchor n="SS.4.4.28-n1"/> aṇutailadravyebhyo niṣpādyata ity
                        aṇutailaṃ | </l>

                    <ab corresp="#SS.4.4.28" type="apparatus">
                        <list type="Emendation">
                            <item xml:lang="en" corresp="#SS.4.4.28-n1">We emend <foreign
                                    xml:lang="sa">-danta-</foreign> in witness H to
                                    <foreign xml:lang="sa">datta</foreign> since this is
                                the reading of the parallel passage in the <title
                                    xml:lang="sa">Aṣṭāṅgasaṅgraha</title> (cikitsāsthāna
                                23.18). But the meaning of the compound remains
                                obscure.</item>
                        </list>
                    </ab>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.4.29">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.4.29</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athavā mahāpañcamūlīkāṣṭhair bbahubhir apadahyāvanipradeśam
                        ekarātram upaśānte 'gnāv apohya bhasmanirvvṛtām bhūmim
                        vidārigandhādisiddhena tailaghaṭaśatenāvasicyaikarātram avasthāpya
                        tato yāvān pāṃśuḥ snigdhaḥ syāt tāvān grāhayitvodake mahati kaṭāhe
                        'bhyāsiñcet | tatra yat tailam uttiṣṭhet tat pāṇibhyām ādāya
                        svanuguptan nidadhyāt | tat tailam
                        vātaharauṣadhakvāthamāṃsarasakṣīrāmlabhāgasahasreṇa sahasrapākam
                        vipacet || yāvatā kālena śaknuyāt paktum prativāpaś cātra
                        haimavatā dakṣiṇāpathagāś cāśvagandhā vātaghnāni ca | tasmin
                        siddhyati śaṅkhān ādhmāpayec chatran dhārayed dundubhīs tāḍayet
                        vālavyajanaiś ca vyajet | tataḥ sādhusiddham avatārya sauvarṇe
                        rājate vā kumbhe nidadhyāt | tad etat sahasrapākam aprativāravīyaṃ
                        rājārhan tailam | evam bhāgaśata<pc> </pc>pakvaṃ śatapākam iti
                        śataṃ pākam iti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.4.30">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.4.30</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         gandharvvahastāṭa<pc> </pc>rūṣaka<pc> </pc>muṣkaka<pc> </pc>naktamāla<pc> </pc>pūtīka<pc> </pc>citrakāṇām
                        pattrāṇy āhṛtyārddrāṇi lavaṇena sahodūkhale saṃkṣudya snehaghaṭe
                        prakṣipyālipya gośakṛdbhir ddāhayet | etat patralavaṇam upadiśanti
                        vātarogeṣu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.4.31">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.4.31</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         evaṃ snuhākāṇḍavārttākulavaṇān saṃkṣudya pūrṇṇaghaṭe
                        sarppistailavasāmajjānaḥ prakṣipyālipya pūrvvavad dahet | etat
                        snehalavaṇam upadiśanti vātarogeṣu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.4.32">

                        etad eva viṃśativargaṃ saphalamūlapatraśākham ārdram āhṛtya
                        lavaṇena saha saṃsṛjya pūrvvavad dagdhvā kṣārakalpena parisrāvya
                        vipacet |<anchor n="SS.4.4.32-n1"/> prativāpaś cātra pippalyādir |
                        etat kalyāṇakan nāma lavaṇam vātaroge

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.5.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.5.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dvividhaṃ vātaraktam uttānam avagāḍhaṃ cety eke bhāṣante
                            ||<anchor n="SS.4.5.3-n1"/> tat tu na samyak | kasmāt |
                        kuṣṭhavad uttānam bhūtvā kālāntareṇāvagāḍhībhavati | tasmād
                        dvitvasaṃkhyā hīyate | </l>

                    <ab corresp="#SS.4.5.3" type="apparatus">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.5.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.5.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra balavadvigrahādibhir vviśeṣaiḥ prakupitasya vāyor
                        ggurūṣṇādhyaśanaśīlasya duṣṭaśoṇitam mārgam āvṛtya vātena
                        sahaikībhūtaṃ yugapad vātaśoṇitanimittāṃ vedanāñ janayati | tad
                        vātaśoṇitam ity ācakṣate | tat tu pūrvvaṃ hastapādayor avasthānaṅ
                        kṛtvā paścād dehe visarppati | tasya pūrvvarūpāṇi toda<pc
                            > </pc>dāha<pc> </pc>kaṇḍū<pc> </pc>śopha<pc
                            > </pc>stambha<pc> </pc>tvakpāruṣya<pc> </pc>sirā<pc
                            > </pc>snāyu<pc> </pc>dhamanī<pc> </pc>spandana<pc
                            > </pc>sakthi<pc> </pc>daurbbalyāni tathā
                        śyāvāruṇaraktamaṇḍalotpattir akasmāc ca
                        pādatalāṅguligulphamaṇibandheṣv eṣām utpattir bbhavati |
                        tatrāpratisāriṇo 'pacāriṇaś ca rogaḥ pravyakto bhavati | tasya
                        lakṣaṇam uktaṃ | tatrāpy apratikāriṇo vaikalyam bhavati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.5.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.5.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         prāyaśaḥ sukumārāṇām mithyāhāravihāriṇāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sthūlānāṃ sukhināñ cāpi kupyate vātaśoṇitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.5.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.5.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra
                        prāṇakṣayapipāsājvaramūrcchāśvāsastambhārocakānavaśīryamāṇaṃ
                        saṅkocair anupadrutam balavantam ātmavantam upakaraṇavantañ
                        copakramet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.5.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.5.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrādāv eva bahuvātarūkṣāmlānāṅgād ṛte mārggāvaraṇakaṃ
                        duṣṭaśoṇitam asakṛd alpālpam avasiñced vātakopabhayāt tato
                        vamanādibhir upakramair upapādya saṃsṛṣṭabhaktavātaprabale
                        purāṇaghṛtaṃ pāyayet | ajākṣīraṃ vārddhatailaṃ madhukākṣayayuktaṃ
                        śṛgālavinnāsiddham vā śarkkarāmadhumadhuraṃ | śuṇṭhīkaśerusiddham
                        vā |
                        śyāmārāsnāsuṣavīśṛgālavinnāpīluśatāvarīśvadaṃṣṭrādvipañcamūlakvāthāṣṭaguṇasiddhena
                        vā payasā
                        meṣaśṛṅgīśvadaṃṣṭrāmadhunāgabalābhadradāruvacāsurabhikalkapratīvāpan
                        tailam vā pācayitvā pānādiṣūpayuñjyāt |
                        śatāvarīmayūrakadhavakamadhukakṣīravidārībalātibalātṛṇapañcamūlīkvāthasiddham
                        vā | kākolyādiprativāpaṃ | balātailam vā śatapākam iti |
                        vātaharamūlasiddhena ca payasā amlair vvā pariṣekaṅ kurvvīta ||
                        tatra cūrṇṇiteṣu yavagodhūmatilamudgamāṣeṣu pratyekaśaḥ
                        kākolīkṣīrakākolījīvakarṣabhakabalātibalāśṛgālavinnāmeṣaśṛṅgīpiyālaśarkkarākaśerukāsurabhivacākalkamiśreṣūpanāhārthe
                        sarppistailavasāmajjādugdhasiddhāḥ pañca pāyasā vyākhyātāḥ |
                        snaihikaphalasārotkārikānalapīnamatsyapiśitavaiśavāro vā |
                        bilvapesikātagaradevadārusaralarāsnāhareṇukuṣṭhaśatapuṣpasurādadhimastuyuktam
                        upanāhaḥ | mātuluṅgāmlasaindhavaghṛtamiśramadhuśigrumūlam ālepanaṃ
                        tilakalko veti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.5.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.5.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pittaprabale
                        drākṣārevatakaṭphalapayasyāmadhukacandanakāśmaryakaṣāyam
                        madhumadhuram pāyayet |
                        śatāvarīpaṭolapattratriphalākaṭurohiṇīguḍūcīkaṣāyam vā |
                        madhuratiktakaṣāyasiddhaṃ sarppiḥ |
                        bisamṛṇālabhadraśriyapadmakakaṣāyeṇājākṣīreṇa pariṣekaḥ |
                        kṣīrekṣurasamadhukaśarkkarātaṇḍulodakair vvā |
                        drākṣekṣukaṣāyamiśrair vvā | mastudhānyāmlair jjīvanīyasiddhena vā
                        | sarppiṣā śatadhautena vā śālipiṣṭakaṃ |
                        nalavañjulatālīsaśṛṅgāṭakakaloḍyāgaurīśaivalapadmaprabhṛtibhir vvā
                        dhānyāmlapiṣṭaḥ pradeho ghṛtamiśraḥ ||</l>

                         śleṣmaprabale tv āmalakaharidrākaṣāyam madhumadhuram pāyayet |
                        triphalākaṣāyaṃ vā | madhukaśṛṅgaveraharītakītiktarohiṇīkalkam vā
                        | sakṣaudramūtreṇa toyena harītakīm vā pāyayet |

                        vā mastumūtrasurāśuktāmadhukaśārivāpadmakasiddhe vā

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.5.12">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.5.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvveṣu ca guḍaharītakīm āseveta | pippalyo vā kṣīrapiṣṭāḥ |
                        pañcābhivṛddhyā pibet kṣīrodanāhāro daśarātraṃ | pañcābhivṛddhyā
                        bhūyañ cāpakarṣayet | evam eva yāvatyañ ceti | tad etat
                        pippalīvarddhamānakam ācakṣate || etad dhi
                        vātaśoṇitaviṣamajvarārocakapāṇḍurogodarārśaḥśvāsakāsaśoṣāgnisādahṛdrogān
                        upahanti | pradehaḥ
                        sahācandanamūrvvāpiyālaśatāvarīkaśerukāsahadevāpadmakamadhukaśatapuṣpākuṣṭhāyavāgūpāṭhaḥ
                        |ni śailepakāṭarūṣakabalātibalājīvantīkalko vā kṣīrayuktaḥ |
                        kāśmaryamadhukatarppaṇakalko vā ghṛtamaṇḍayuktaḥ |
                        madhūcchiṣṭaśārivāsarjjarasamadhukamadhuravarggakṣīrasiddham vā
                        piśutailam iti ||
                        purāṇaghṛtamāmalakasaralavipakvaśarkkarāmadhumadhuraṃm pānārthe |
                        jīvanīyasiddhaṃ pariṣekārthe || suṣavīkvāthasiddhaṃ vā |
                        balātailaṃ siddhaṃ pariṣekāvagāhabastibhojanārtham iti |
                        śāliṣaṣṭikayavagodhūmānnam upaseveta | payasā jāṅgalarasena
                        mudgayūṣeṇa vānamlena śoṇitamokṣaṇañ cocchritadoṣagrahaṇena
                        vamanavirecanāsthāpanānuvāsanakarmmāseveta || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.5.13"/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.5.18">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.5.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāpatākinam asrastākṣam avakrabhruvam astabdhāṅgulam asvedanam
                        avepanam apralāpinam iti pāṭhaḥ akhaṭvāyātinam abahirāyāminañ
                        copakramet | tatra prāg eva snehābhyaktaṃ svinnaśarīram avapīḍena
                        tīkṣṇenopakramet śiraḥśuddhyarthaṃ | athānantaram
                        vidārigandhādikvāthekṣurasakṣīradadhivipakvaṃ sarppir accham
                        pāyayet | tathā nātimātram vāyuḥ prasarati | tato bhadradārvādīni
                        vātaghnāny anyāni cāṅgāny āhṛtya yavakolakulatthāṃś ca
                        sānūpodakamāṃsāny ekataḥ kvāthyam ādāya kaṣāyam amlakṣīraiḥ
                        sahonmiśrya sarppistailavasāmajjābhiḥ saha pacet
                        madhurakapratīvāpaṃ | tad etat traivṛtam apatānakinām
                        pariṣekābhyaṅgapānabhojanānuvāsananasyeṣu vidadhyād yathoktaiś ca
                        svedavidhānaiḥ svedayed balīyasi vāte sukhoṣṇapariṣekapūrṇṇe
                        nikhanet taptāyām vā | rathākāracullyāṃ | kṛsaravaiśavārapāyasair
                        vvā svedayen
                        mūlakoruvūkasphūrjjakārkkasaptalāśaṅkhinīsvarasasiddham apatānakim
                        pariṣekādiṣu yojyam abhuktavatām pītam amlan dadhi maricayuktam
                        apatānakam apahanti | sarppis tailavasāmajjā vā etac
                        chuddhavātāpatānakavidhim uktaṃ | saṃsṛṣṭe saṃsṛṣṭaṅ karttavyaṃ |
                        vegāntareṣu cāvapīḍān dadyāt |
                        tāmracūḍakarkkaṭakakṛṣṇamatsyaśiśumārarasāñ cāvekṣyate | kṣīrāni
                        vātaharasiddhāni | yavakolakulatthamūlakadadhighṛtatailasiddhāṃ
                        yavāgūṃ | snehavirecanāsthāpanānuvāsanaiś cenan daśarātram
                        āgatavegam upacaret | vātavyādhicikitsitañ cāvekṣyeta |
                        rakṣākarmma ca kuryāt | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.5.19">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.5.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pakṣāghātopadrutam amlānagātraṃ sarujam ātmavantañ copakramet |
                        tatra prāg eva snehasvedopapannaṃ | mṛdunā śodhanena
                        saṃśodhyānuvāsyāsthāpya ca yathākālam ākṣepakavidhānenopacaret |
                        vaiśeṣikamastiṣkaśirobastibhir iti | aṇutailam abhyaṅgārthe |
                        sālvalam upanāhārthe | balātailam anuvāsanārthe | evam atandritas
                        trīṃś caturo vā māsāṅ kriyām āseveta || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.5.20">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.5.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         manyāstambhe 'pyetad eva vidhānaṃ, viśeṣato vātaśleṣmaharair
                        nasyai rūkṣasvedaiś copacaret || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.5.21"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.5.22">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.5.22</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ardditāturam balavantam upakaraṇavantañ ca
                        vātavyādhividhānenopacaret | vaiśeṣikaś ca
                        mastiṣkaśirobastinasyadhūpopanāhanāḍīsvedais | tataḥ
                        satṛṇamahatpañcamūlīm āhṛtya dviguṇodake kṣīre
                        kvāthyakṣīrāvaśiṣṭam avatārya parisrāvya tailaprasthenonmiśrya
                        punar agnāv adhisritya vipacet tatas tailaṃ kṣīrānugatam avatārya
                        śītībhūtam mathnīyāt | tad etat kṣīratailam ardditānām
                        pānādiṣūpayojyam iti | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.5.23">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.5.23</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         gṛdhrasīviścañcīkroṣṭukaśīrṣapaṅgukalāyakhañjavātakaṇṭakapādadāhapādaharṣa
                        avabāhukabādhiryadhamanīvāteṣu yathoktasirāvyadhaṃ
                        kṛtvānyatrāvabāhukād vātavyādhicikitsitam avekṣyeta | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.5.24">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.5.24</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         karṇṇamūle tu śṛṅgaverarasair mmadhukatailasaṃsṛṣṭaḥ
                        saindhavopahitaḥ sukhoṣṇaḥ karṇṇayor ddeyaḥ |
                        ajamūtramadhukatailāni vā |
                        mātuluṅgadāḍimatintiḍīkarasamūtrasiddham vā tailam |
                        suktasurātakramūtrasiddham vā nāḍīsvedaiś ca svedayet |
                        vātavyādhicikitsāñ cāvekṣyeta || bhūyaś cottare vakṣyāmaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.5.25">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.5.25</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tūnīpratitūnyoḥ snehaṃ lavaṇam uṣṇodakena pāyayet |
                        pippalyādicūrṇṇam vā | hiṅguyavakṣārapragāḍham vā sarppiḥ |
                        bastibhiś copakramet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.5.26">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.5.26</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ādhmāne tv avatarppaṇaṃ pāṇitāpaphalavarttikriyādīpanapācanāni
                        kuryac chodhanabastyupayogaś ca | pratyādhmāne
                        charddanāpatarppaṇadīpanīyāni | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.5.27">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.5.27</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         aṣṭhīlāpratyaṣṭhīlayor ggulmābhyantaravidradhikriyāvibhāga iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.5.28">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.5.28</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         hiṅgutrikaṭukavacājamodadhānyājagandhādāḍimatintiḍīkapāṭhācittrakacavyāsaindhavaviḍasauvarccalayavakṣārasuvarccikāpippalīmūlāmlavetasaśaṭhīpuṣkarahapuṣājājīpathyāḥ
                        sañcūrṇṇya mātuluṅgāmlena bahuśaḥ paribhāvyākṣamātrā guḍikāḥ
                        kārayet tataḥ prātar ekaikām vātarogī bhakṣayed eṣa khalu yogo
                        gulmaśvāsakāsārocakahṛdrogādhmānapārśvodarabastiśūlānāhamūtrakṛcchrārśaḥplīhodarapāṇḍurogān
                        apahanti tūnīpratitūnīṣu cātyartham upayujyate ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.5.29">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.5.29</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavanti cātra||
                        <caesura/>
                         kevalo doṣayukto vā dhātūn anugato 'nilaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vijñeyo lakṣaṇonyām̐ś ca cikitsyaś cāvirodhataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.5.30">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.5.30</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rujāvantaṃ ghanaṃ śītaṃ śophamedoyuto 'nilaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         karoti yasya tam vaidyaḥ śophavat samupācaret || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.5.31">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.5.31</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaphamedoyuto vāyur ūrū saṃśrayate yadā |
                        <caesura/>
                         tadāṅgamarddastaimityaṃ romaharṣarujājvaraiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.5.32">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.5.32</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nidrayā cārdditastabdhau śītalāv apravepanau |
                        <caesura/>
                         gurukāv asthirāv ūrū pārakyāv iva varttate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.5.33">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.5.33</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tadūrūstambham ity āhur āḍhyavātam athāpare |
                        <caesura/>
                         sukhāmbunā pibet tatra cūrṇṇaṃ ṣaṇḍharaṇan naraḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.5.34">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.5.34</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         hitam uṣṇāmbunā tadvat pippalyādigaṇe kṛtaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         lihyād vā traiphalācūrṇṇaṃ kṣaudreṇa kaṭukāyutaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.5.35">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.5.35</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mūtrair vvā gugguluṃ śreṣṭham pibed vāpi śilājatuṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         so 'pahanti kaphākrāntaṃ samedaskam prabhañjanaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.5.36">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.5.36</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         hṛdrogam aruciṃ gulman tathābhyantaravidradhiṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sakṣāramūtrān svedām̐ś ca rūkṣāṇy utsādanāni ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.5.37">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.5.37</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kuryād dihyāc ca mūtrāḍhyaiḥ karañjaphalasarṣapaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhojyā purāṇāḥ śyāmākāḥ kodravoddālakādayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.5.38">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.5.38</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         jāṅgalair akṛtair mmāṃsaiḥ śākaiś cālavaṇair hitaiḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.5.39">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.5.39</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         parikṣīṇau yadā syātāṃ bhūyiṣṭhaṅ kaphamedasī ||
                        <caesura/>
                         tadā snehādikaṅ karmma punar atrāvacārayed iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.6.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.6.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto 'rśasāṃ cikitsitamvyākhyāmyāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.6.2">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.6.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atha khalu vatsasuśrutaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.6.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.6.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         caturvvidho 'rśasāṃ sādhanopāyaḥ | tad yathābheṣajaṃ kṣāro 'gniḥ
                        śastra i || <space quantity="5" unit="akṣara"/> || ti |
                        tatrācirakālajātāny alpadoṣaliṅgopadravāni bheṣajasādhyāni |
                        mṛduprasṛtāvagāḍhānyuchritāni kṣāreṇa |
                        karkkaśasthirapṛthukaṭhināny agninā | atanumūlāny uchritāni
                        kledavanti ca śastreṇa | tatra bheṣajasādhyānām arśasāmadṛśyānāñ
                        ca bheṣajam bhavati | kṣārāgni śastrasādhyānāṃ kṣārāgniśastrāṇi ca
                        | teṣām vidhānam upadhārayasva | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.6.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.6.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatravalavantam arśobhir upadrutam
                        upasnigdhapari<sic>sni</sic>nnam anilavedanābhivrddhiśamanārthaṃ
                        snigdham analpam annadravabhuktavantaṃ samveśya śucau sādhāraṇe
                        deśe vyabhre kāle same phalake pratyād ity agudam anyasyotsaṅge
                        niṣarṇṇaṃ pūrvvakāyam uttānam unnatakaṭīkaṃ yastrasāṭakena
                        parikṣipyagrīvāsakthir upari karmmabhiḥ suparigṛhītaṃ kārayitvā
                        tato 'smai ghṛtābhyaktaṃ yantramṛjvanumukhaṃ śannaiḥ praṇidhāya
                        praviṣṭe cārśo 'bhivīkṣyasalākayotpīḍya picuplotayor anyatareṇa
                        pramṛjyākṣāram pātayet | pātayitvā pāṇinā yantradvāram pidhāya
                        vākchatamātram upekṣeta | tataḥ pramṛjya kṣāralavaṇañ cāvekṣya
                        punaḥ pratisārayet | atharśaḥ pakvajāmvūprakāśam abhisamīkṣyo
                        vasannamīṣattataḥ | apāvarttayet | dhānyāmladadhimastuśuktānām
                        anyatamena | tato yaṣṭīm adhukamiśreṇasarppiṣā nirvvāpya yantram
                        upanīyotthāpy āturasuṣṇodake 'vagāhyaśītābhir adbhiḥ pariṣecayet |
                        aśītābhir adbhir ity eke | tato nivātam agāram preveśyācārikam
                        upadiśet | sāvaśeṣam punar ddāhayet | tatra saptarātrāccaikaikam
                        upakrāmet | tato vāmāt tataḥ pṛṣṭhajāgrajam iti | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.6.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.6.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra vātaśleṣmanimittāny agnikṣārābhyāṃ sādhayet | kṣāreṇaiva
                        pittaraktasamutthāni | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.6.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.6.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra vātānulomyamann ebhir uciragnidīptilāghavam
                        valavarṇṇotpattir mmanas tuṣṭir iti samyagdagdhaliṅgāni |
                        atidagdhe tu gudāvaraṇan dāhodjvaraḥ pipāsā śoṇitātipravṛttis tan
                        nimittāś copadravā bhavanti | dhyāmālpatākaṇḍūn anilavaiguṇyañ ca
                        hīnadagdhe |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.6.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.6.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ma hānti vā prāṇavatasthitvād ahet | nirgatāni cātyarthan
                        doṣaparipūrṇṇāgatāni snehābhyaṅgasvedopanāha visrāvaṇālepanair
                        upacaret | pravṛttraktāni vā pitta raktavidhānena |
                        bhinnavarccāṃsi cātīsāravidhānena | vaddhavarccāṃsi
                        codāvarttavidhāneneti | eṣa sarvvasthānagatānām arśasān
                        dahanakalpaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.6.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.6.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         āsādya darvvīkū rccasalākānām anyatamena kṣāram pātayet |
                        bhraṣṭagudasya tuvinā yantraṃ kṣārādikarmma prayuñjīta | sarvveṣu
                        ca śāliṣaṣṭikayavagodhūmānnaṃ sarppiḥ snigdham upaseveta | payasā
                        nimvayūṣeṇa paṭolayūṣeṇa vā | yathādoṣair
                        vvāstūkataṇḍulīyakajīvantyupodakāśca
                        valavālamūlakaśaṇacuñcucillīnām anyatamena | yaccānyad api
                        snighdamagnidīpanamarśoghnaṃ sṛṣṭamūtrapurīṣañ ca tad upaseveta
                        |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.6.9">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.6.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dagdheṣu cārśasastv analasandhukṣaṇārthaṃ snehādī sāmānyato
                        viśeṣataś ca kriyāyatham āseveta | &#x1145b; sarppīṃṣi ca
                        vātaharadīpanīyasiddhāni hiṃgvādīnāṃ cūrṇṇaiḥ pratisaṃsṛjya pivet
                        | pittārśas supṛthakparṇṇyādīnāṅ kaṣāyeṇa dīpanīyaprativāpaṃ
                        sarppiḥ pivet | śoṇitārśassu muruṃgyādīnāṅ kaṣāyaiḥ | śleṣmārśassu
                        surasādīnāṅ kaṣāyaiḥ | upadravām̐ś ca yathāsvam upacaret | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.6.10">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.6.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         parañ ca yatnamāsthāya gude śastrānyavacārayet | ta dvibhramāc
                        chāṇḍhyaśophadāhamadamūrcchāṭopānāhātīsārapravāhaṇāni bhavanti |
                        maraṇam vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.6.11">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.6.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ata ūrddhvaṃ yantrapramāṇam upadekṣyāmaḥ | tatra yantraṃ lauhan
                        dāntaṃ śāṃrggam vā rkṣam vā | gostanākārañ caturaṅgulāyatam
                        pañcāṅgulapariṇāhaṃ | nārīṇān talāyatam ity eke | tad dvichidraṃ |
                        darśanārtham ekaśchidran tu karmmaṇi | ekachidre hi śastrā
                        gnikṣārāṇām atikramo na bhavati | chidrapramāṇaṃ tu
                        tryaṅgulāyatamaṅguṣṭhodaravistāraṃ yadaṅgulamavaśiṣṭaṃ tat
                        syāddvyaṅgulam adhastāduparyarddhāṅgulochritam
                        arddhāṅguṣṭhoparivṛttakarṇṇikam eṣa yantrākṛtisamāsaḥ ||ch||</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.6.12">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.6.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ata ūrddhvamarśasāmālepo vakṣyāmaḥ || snuhākṣīrayuktaṃ
                        haridrācūrṇṇam ālepaḥ prathamaḥ |
                        kukkuṭapurīṣaguñjāharidrāpippalīcūrṇṇ am iti gomūtrapiṣṭo dvitīyaḥ
                        | dantīcitrakasuvarccikākalko gomūtrayuktastṛtīyaḥ |
                        pippalīsaindhavakuṣṭhaśirīṣakalko 'rkakṣīrayuktaś ca caturthaḥ ||
                        kāsī
                        saharitālasaindhavāśvamārakaviḍaṅgapūtīkakṛtavedhanājambukāśvakottamakiṇihīsnuhāpayassu
                        ca | tailam vipakvamabhyañjanenārśasaḥ sātayeyur iti || || ṃ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.6.13">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.6.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ata ūrddham adṛśyeṣv arśassu yogānyapanayārthaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ|| tatra
                        guḍaharītakīm āseveta brahmacārī | gomūtradroṇasiddham vā
                        harītakīśatam upaseveta ya thāvalaṃ kṣaudreṇa | apāmārggamūlam vā
                        taṇḍulodakena | śatāvarīmūlakalkam vā kṣīreṇa | cittrakacūrṇṇam vā
                        sīdhunā | madhurārddhabhallātakacūrṇṇayuktam vā śaktūn | la vaṇo
                        takreṇa | kalase vāntaś cittrakamūlakalkalipte niṣiktaṃ takram
                        anamlam pānabhojaneṣūpayuñjīta | eṣa eva bhārggyāsphātāguḍūcīṣu
                        takrakalpaḥ| pippalīpippalīmūlaṃ viḍaṅgaśuṇṭhīharītakīṣu vā |
                        pūrvvavad eva niranno vā takram aharaharmmāsamāseveta |
                        śṛṅgaverapunarṇṇasiddhaṃ vā payaḥ | kraṭajamūlatva kphāṇitam vā
                        pippalyādipratīvāpaṃ kṣaudreṇa vātavyādhyoktaṃ hiṃgvādivaṭake
                        upaseveta | takrāhārakṣīrāhāro vā | citrakamūlakaṣāyasiddhaṃ vā
                        kulmāṣām bhakṣa yet | palāśataruṇasiddham vā
                        pāṭalyapāmārggavṛhatīpalāśakṣāram vā parisrutam
                        aharaharghṛtayuktaṃ | kuṭajacandākamūlakalkam vā | takreṇa |
                        kṣārodakasiddham vā sa rppiḥ pippalyādiprativāpaṃ |
                        kṛṣṇatilaprakuñcam vā śītatoyānupānam prātaḥ prātar upaseveta |
                        evam ebhir nnavam varddhate 'gniś ca bhavati arśāṃsi copaśāmyati | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.6.14">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.6.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dvi pañcamūladantīcittrakapathyānān tulāmāhṛtya jaladroṇe ci
                        pācayet | pādāvaśiṣṭaṅ kaṣāyam ādāya suśītaṅ guḍatulayā
                        sahonmiśrya ghṛtabhājane niṣicya yavapalleplave samupekṣeta tataḥ
                        prātaḥ prātar mmātrām pāyayet |
                        tenārśasograhaṇīdoṣapāṇḍurogaudāvarttaśvāsakā sā rocakāgni
                        daurvvalyāni na bhavanti || ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.6.15">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.6.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pippalīmaricaviḍaṃgailavālukalodhrāṇāṃ dvipalikān bhāgān
                        indravāruṇyāḥ pañcapalāni harītakyāmalakapitthaphalānāṃ daśa daśa
                        etadaikadhyaṃ jalacaturdroṇe vi pācya pādāvaśeṣaṃ viśrāvya suśītaṃ
                        guḍatulādvayonnmiśrya ghṛtabhājane nikṣicya pakṣamātram upakṣiyeta
                        yavapalle tataḥ prātaḥ prātar yathāvalam upayuñjī ta | eṣa
                        khalvariṣṭo
                        'rśograhaṇīplīhahṛtpāṇḍurogaśophakuṣṭhagulmodarakrimiharo
                        valavarṇṇakaraś ceti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.6.16">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.6.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra vātaprāyeṣu snehasvedasnehavirecanāsthā
                        panānuvāsanamapratisiddhaṃ | pittajeṣu virecanam eva | saṃśamanaṃ
                        raktajeṣu | kaphajeṣu śṛṅgaverakulatthopayogo
                        yathāsvauṣadhasiddhaṃ sarvvajeṣu || ṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.6.17">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.6.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ata ūrddhvam bhallātakavidhānam upadekṣyāmaḥ || bhallātakān
                        paripakvān anupahatān āhṛtya tata ekamādāya tridhā caturddhā
                        chedayitvā kaṣāyakalpena vipācya tasya kaṣāyasya śuktimanuṣṇāṃ
                        ghṛtābhyaktatālvoṣṭhajihvaḥ prātaḥ prātar upaseveta | aparāhṇe
                        kṣīrasarppirodana ity āhāraḥ | evam ekaikam varddhayed yāvat pañca
                        | tataś corddha pañca pañcābhivarddhayed āsatād iti | prāpya ca
                        śata śatam apakarṣayed bhūyaḥ pañca pañca yāvat pañceti |
                        pañcebhyas ca yāvadeka iti | evaṃ bhallātakasahasradvayam upayujya
                        sarvvābhir vvimukto valavānn arogaḥ śatāyur bbhavati | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.6.18">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.6.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhallātakamajjebhyaḥ snehamādāyāpakṛṣṭadoṣaḥ pratisaṃsṛṣṭabhaktaḥ
                        | nivātam agāraṃ praviśya yathāvalam upayuñjīta | tasmi n jīrṇṇe
                        kṣīrasarppirodana ity āhāraḥ | evaṃ māsam upayujya māsatrayam
                        upadiṣṭāhāro rakṣed ātmānan tataḥ sarvvopatāpānapahṛtya varṇṇavān
                        balavāñ chravaṇa grahaṇadhāraṇaśaktisampanno varṣaśatāyurbbhavati
                        | māsi māsi ca prayoge varṣaśataṃ varṣaśatamāyuṣo 'bhivṛddhir
                        bbhavati | evan daśamāsān upayujya varṣa sahasrāyur bbhavati ||
                        bhavanti cātra ślokāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.6.19">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.6.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         arśāṃsi sarvvāṇi sadā , vrkṣakāruṣkarau ghnataḥ | yathā sarvvāṇi
                        kuṣṭhāni gāyatryaśanapādayoḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.6.20">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.6.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣārāgninā nivarttante dṛśyānyarśāṃsi sarvvadā | rajanyo
                        nābhivarttante pramehā iva ṣoḍaśa ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.6.21">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.6.21</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ghṛtānidīpanīyāni lehāyakṛtayaḥ surāḥ | asavāś ca prayoktavyā
                        vīkṣyadoṣasamuchreyaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.6.22">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.6.22</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vegāvarodhastrīpṛṣṭhayānāny 7 utku dukāsanaṃ |
                        yathāsvandoṣalañcannam arśasī parivarjjayed iti || cikitsāṣaṭ ||
                    </l>

                        abhyaktam abhuktavantaṃ sninnaśarīraṃ kṛtamaṅgalasvastivācanam
                        agropaharaṇīyoktena vidhinānena sasambhṛtasambhāram āśvāsya tato
                        valavantam aviklavam ājānusame phalake prāgupaveśya puru ṣan
                        tasyotsaṅge niṣaṇṇapūrvakāyamuttānaṃ unnatakaṭīkaṃ
                        vastracumbhalakopaviṣṭaṃ saṅkucatijānukurpparamitareṇa
                        sahāvavaddhaṃ | sūtrakena śāṭakena vātataḥ
                        svabhyaktanābhipradeśapārśvasyāvamṛdya muṣṭinā pīḍayed adho nābher
                        yāvad aśma ryadhaḥ pratipanneti | tataḥ snehābhyakta kliptanakho
                        vāmahastapradeśinī madhyamāṅgulyau praṇidhāyānusevanīm āsādya
                        prayatnavalābhyāṃ meḍhragudayor antaramānayitvā
                        nirvvalīkamanāyatanamaviṣamañ ca basti sanniveśya bhṛśamutpīḍayed

                        <label xml:lang="en">4.7.33</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tataḥ sevanyāḥ savye pārśve sevanī yavamātreṇāvamucyāvacārayec
                        chastraṃ | aśmarīpramāṇād dakṣiṇato vā kriyā saukaryahetor ity eke
                        | yathā na bhidyate na vacūrṇṇyate vā tathā prayateta ||
                        taccūrṇṇam alpam apy evasthitaṃ hi punaḥ parivṛddham eti | tasmāt
                        mamagrām agravakrenādadīta | strīṇān tu bastiḥ pārśvagato
                        garbbhāsayasannicayas tasmā t tāsām mutsaṅgavac chastraṃ pātayet
                        || atonyathā khalvāsām mūtrasrāvī vraṇo bhavati || puruṣasya vā
                        mūtraprasekakṣaṇanād aśmarī vraṇādṛte bhinnabastir ekadhā dvidhā
                        vā na bhavati | dvidhā bhinnabastikāśmarīko pi na sidhyati |
                        aśmarīnimittaś ca vraṇam ekadhā bhinnabasti vidhinā jīvati
                        śastrakriyābhyāṃ śastravihitāc chedābhiṣyandaparivṛddhatvāc ca
                        śalyasya jīved iti | uddhṛtaśalyam uṣṇodakadroṇyāṃ cāvagāhya
                        svedayet tathāhi bastir asṛjā na pūryate |</l>

                        <caesura/>
