                <div n="19" type="adhyāya">

                    <head>[Adhyāya 19]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.1"> athāto vṛddhyupadaṃśaślīpadānāṃ cikitsitaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.3"> antravṛddhim ṛte ye 'nye vṛddhayas teṣu
                        varjayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         vegāghātaṃ pṛṣṭhayānaṃ vyāyāmaṃ maithunaṃ tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.4"> anaśanaṃ cātyaśanam adhyaśanam atho guruḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrādito vātavṛddhau trivṛtāsnigdham āturam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.5"> sninnañ caiva yathānyāyam pāyayīta virecanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kośāmratilvakair aṇḍaphalatailāni vā naraḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.6"> sakṣīram vā pibet māsaṃ tailam eraṇḍasambhavaṃ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         tataḥ kāle 'nilaghnānāṃ kvāthaiḥ kalkaiś ca buddhimān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.7"> nirūhayen nirūḍhañ ca bhuktavantaṃ rasodanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yaṣṭīmadhukasiddhena tatas tailena yojayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.8"> svedopanāhau kuryāc ca pradehām̐ś cānilāpahān |
                        <caesura/>
                         vidagdham pācayitvā vā sevanīm parivarjjayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.9"> bhindyād bhitvā ca matimān yathoktaṃ kramam
                        ācaret |
                        <caesura/>
                         pittagranthikramaṅ kuryād apakvam pittasambhave || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.10"> śastropapannam bhitvā vā śodhayen
                        madhusarppiṣā |
                        <caesura/>
                         śuddhe ca copaśaṅ kalkaṃ dadyāt tailan tu yaddhitaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.11"> muhur muhur jjalaukābhiḥ śoṇitaṃ raktaje haret
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         pibed virecanam vāpi śarkkarākṣaudrasaṃyutaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.12"> pittagranthikramaṃ kuryād āme pakve ca raktaje
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         śleṣmavṛddhim uṣṇavīryair mmūtrapiṣṭais tu lepayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.13"> pītadārukaṣāyañ ca pibet mūtreṇa saṃyutaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vimlāpanād ṛte cāpi śleṣmagranthikrame hitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.14"> pakvabhinne viśuddhyarthan tailaṃ deyam
                        vijānatā |
                        <caesura/>
                         sumanāruṣkarāṅkoṭhasaptaparṇṇeṣu sādhitaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.15"> svedyam medaḥ samutthan tu lepayet surasādinā
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         śirovirekadravyair vvā sukhoṣṇair mmūtrasaṃyutaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.16"> svinnam vāveṣṭa paṭṭena samāśvāsya ca mānavaṃ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         rakṣamūlaṃ sevanīñ ca vṛddhipattreṇa dārayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.17"> medaḥ samuddhṛtya tato dadyāt kāsīsasaindhave
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         badhnīyāc ca yathoddiṣṭaṃ śuddhe tailañ ca dāpayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.18"> manaḥśilālalavaṇaiḥ siddhamāruḥkareṣu ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         svedyamūtranimittan tu vastrapaṭṭena veṣṭayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.19"> sevanyām pārśvato 'dhastād vidhyed

                        <caesura/>
                         athātrodaravan nāḍīn dattvā visrāvayed bhiṣak || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.20"> mūtranāḍīm athoddhṛtya sthavikābandham ācaret

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.20.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athātaḥ kṣudrarogāṇā cikitsitam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.20.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrādita eva jagañ jalāyukābhir grāhayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         kalkaiś cālepayet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.20.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śyāmāpāṭhālāṅgalīkalkair vā pakvām vā pākavidhānenopacaret ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.5-6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.20.5-6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yavaprakhyām ambālajīṃ panasikām pāṣāṇagardabhaṅ kacchapikāñ ca
                        svedayitvā suradārukuṣṭhaharitālamanaḥśilākalkair ālepayet |
                        pakvāṃ vā pākavidhānenopacaret || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.7-8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.20.7-8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vivṛtām indraviddhāṃ gardabhikāṃ jālagardabham irivellikāṃ
                        gandhanāmāṃ kakṣām visphoṭāṃś ca pittavisarpavidhānenopacaret |
                        pakvāṃś ca madhurauṣadhasiddhena sarpiṣā ropayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.9-10">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.20.9-10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         cipyān tūṣṇāmbunā pariṣecyotkṛtyāpanayec cakratailenābhyajya
                        sarjarasarasacūrṇṇenāvacūrṇṇya bandhenopacared evam aśakyam agninā
                        dahet | madhurauṣadhasiddhena ca tailenopacaret || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.11">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.20.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         anuśayīṃ śleṣma vidradhivad upacaret | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.12-13">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.20.12-13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vidārikām abhyajya parisvedya vimlāpayet |
                        bilvamūlanāgavṛttikāvarṣābhūkalkaiś cālepayet | vraṇabhāvaṇam
                        āpannaṃ vā madhurakaṣāyauṣadhasiddhena tailena ropayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.14"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.15"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.16"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.17-18">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.20.17-18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śarkarārbudam medorbudavad upacaret ||
                        <caesura/>
                         kacchūvicarcikārakaśāsu kuṣṭhavat pratīkāro viśeṣatas tu
                        śatāhvāsarṣapakalkair ālepayet | siddhārthakadāruharidrākalkair vā
                        | saralātailena vā | kaṭukauṣadhasiddhenābhyañjyāt |
                        naktamālatailena vā |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.19">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.20.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pakvāṃś ca pakvavidhānenopacaret ||
                        <caesura/>
                         pādadāryān tu sirām vidhyet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.20">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.20.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pādau snehasvedopapannā madhūcchiṣṭaghṛtavasāmajjābhir
                        yavakṣāramiśrair ālepayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.21-22">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.20.21-22</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         alase tv āmlakāñjikasiktau caraṇau
                        paṭolapicumardatilakāsīsarocanākalkair ālepayet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.23">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.20.23</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nidigdhikārasasiddhena ca sarṣapatailenābhyajya
                        kāsīsarocanāmanaḥśilācūrṇṇaiḥ pratisārayet || kadaram uddhṛtya
                        dahet snehena || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.24">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.20.24</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         indralupte tu śirasi sirām vidhā tu ndamanaḥśilāmaricakalkair
                        ālepayet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.25-26">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.20.25-26</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhadradārukalkair vā jātīcitrakakaravīranaktamālakalkasiddhena
                        tailenābhyañjyāt | rasāyanavidhānañ cāsevena | avagāḍhapadaṃ
                        pracchayitvā guñjāphalakalkair bhūyo bhūyaḥ pradihyāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.27-29">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.20.27-29</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śoṇitam avasicya nimbodakena parisicyāśvaviḍrasena
                        lavaṇapragāḍhenālepayet | paṭolapicumardaharidrākalkair vā |
                        madhukotpalatilairaṇḍamārkavapatrair vā | indraluptoktena
                        tailenābhyañjyāt || dāruṇake tu snigdhasvinnasya lalāṭe sirām
                        vyadhet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.30">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.20.30</label>

                        kodravatṛṇakṣaraudakaprakṣālanañ ca || </l>

                        || </l>

                        pratisārayet | agninā vā dahet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.33">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.20.33</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nacchanīlikāvyaṅgeṣu yathābhyāśaṃ lalāṭe sirām visrāvayet | </l>

                        <caesura/>

                        madhughṛtayuktayā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.37-38a">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.20.37-38a</label>

                        siddhārthakavacālodhrasaindhavakalkair vā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.38i"/>

                        <caesura/>
                         parivarttikāṃ tu sarpiṣābhyajya svedayet | vātaghnais tataḥ
                        sninnām upanāhayet | sālvalena veśavāreṇa vā trirātram pañcarātram
                        vā tataḥ svedayitvābhyajya śanaiḥ śanaiś carma samānayaṃ
                        manipatham avapīḍayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.42">
                        <label xml:lang="en">4.20.42</label>

                        āharet || avapāṭikayām apy evaṃ yathādoṣaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.43">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.44">
